The Acharya Institute of Technology is a technological university affiliated with Visvesvaraya Technological University, located in Bangalore, India. It is situated at "In Soldevanahalli, Acharya Dr. Sarvapalli Radhakrishnan Road, Hessarghatta Main Road, Bangalore – 560090". The institute has approximately 700 postgraduate students.
